<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайм.html>тайм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tajm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайм.html>та́йма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайм.html>та́ймы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайм.html>та́ймов</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> half time, half, round

***тайна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йна</a> (1440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">таина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tájna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mystery (something secret or unexplainable)</li>
<li>secret</li>
<li>secrecy</li>
<li>obscurity</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таить.html>таи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайный.html>та́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tájnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>secret</li>
<li>stealthy; surreptitious</li>
<li>vague</li>
<li>privy</li></ol>

***тайфун.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайфун.html>тайфу́н</a> (23462)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">typhoon</i>, probably ultimately of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sinitic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sinitic languages">Sinitic</a></span> origin, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandarin_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Mandarin Chinese">Mandarin</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="cmn">大风</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cmn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dàfēng</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese">Cantonese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">大風</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">daai<sup>6</sup> fung<sup>1</sup></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طوفان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭūfān</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">तूफ़ान</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tūfān</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">توفان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tufân</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайфун.html>тайфу́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tajfún</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайфун.html>тайфу́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайфун.html>тайфу́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайфун.html>тайфу́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">weather</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> typhoon</li></ol>

***так.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> (26)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тако</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tako</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">такъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">takŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tako</i> (adverb), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*takъ</i> (adjective). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">тако</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tako</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Belarusian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">така</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">тако</i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></i>; Slovene <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">tаkо</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">tàk</i>; Czech and Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">tak</i>; Upper and Lower Sorbian <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">tak</i>; Lithuanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tóks</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tokià</i>; and Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tālis</i>. Akin to Old Church Slavonic pronoun <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">тъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tak</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>so, thus
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tak</b> že</i> ― <span class="e-translation">just as</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tak</b> i</i> ― <span class="e-translation">and</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>та́к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ták</b> kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">since, because</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tak</b> i ne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">never</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>like that</li>
<li>so much

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>та́кже</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tákže</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>also, too, as well, likewise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>та́кже</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>прихо́дит</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>tákže</b> prixódit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He too is coming.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in negative constructions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> either, neither, nor</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">takí</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>still, after all, in spite of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> росси́ю</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>takí</b> pojéxala v Rossíju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she went to Russia after all.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таки.html>таки́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>takí</b> ne prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">still, he is in the wrong.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***таков.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таков.html>таков</a> (1980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таков.html>тако́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">takóv</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>such
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочинение.html>сочине́ния</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:таковой.html>таковы́</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsé moí sočinénija <b>takový</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My essays are all like that. / My essays are all the same. (in terms of writing style)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:таковой.html>таковы́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>takový</b> fákty</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>such</b> are the facts</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>талант</a> (2034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">talánt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>talent, gift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zaryvátʹ svoj <b>talánt</b> v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bury one's talent;  to hide one's light under a bushel;  to hide one's talents in a napkin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> man or woman of talent, gifted person, talent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> talent <i>(measure of weight and monetary unit)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талантливый.html>тала́нтливый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">talántlivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***талантливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:талантливый.html>тала́нтливый</a> (3494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">talánt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талантливый.html>тала́нтливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">talántlivyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тала́нтливее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тала́нтливей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тала́нтливейшый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gifted, talented</li>
<li>performed with talent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дарови́тый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">darovítyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одаренный.html>одарённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odarjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***талмуд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:талмуд.html>талму́д</a> (21495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">תלמוד</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">talmud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талмуд.html>талму́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">talmúd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талмуд.html>талму́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талмуд.html>талму́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талмуд.html>талму́дов</a></b>)

***талый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:талый.html>та́лый</a> (13801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tájatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to melt, thaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:талый.html>та́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tályj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thawed; melted; partly melted; slushy (e.g. of snow)</li></ol>

***там.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> (77)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тамо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tamo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tamo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tam</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>there</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>тамбур</a> (7984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>та́мбур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">támbur</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>та́мбура</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>та́мбуры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>та́мбуров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tambour</li>
<li><i>(at the entrance)</i> lobby</li>
<li>vestibule <i>(of a train carriage)</i></li>
<li>chain stitch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышивать.html>вышива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>тамбуром</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyšivátʹ tamburom</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">embroider in chain stitch</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>тамбу́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tambúr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>тамбу́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>тамбу́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамбур.html>тамбу́ров</a></b>)
</p>

***таможня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таможня.html>тамо́жня</a> (8360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тамга</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tamga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">тамға</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tamğa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> "brand, mark").
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таможня.html>тамо́жня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tamóžnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таможня.html>тамо́жни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таможня.html>тамо́жни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таможня.html>тамо́жен</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таможенный.html>тамо́женный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>custom house</li></ol>
